# Synopsis

The troupe is now entirely in Montimer, the forest thickining and then thinning before coming up onto a Castle proper. It is undoubtedly one of the three Montimerian castles built before even Ethan Sedi.

There is some discussion if the party will be staying Inside the Castle vs Outside the Castle. Do the Silverridges perceive the Bennets as an open threat? They split the difference for now: during the tournement, they have rented rooms at a local inn to recover from their trip and participate in the festivies than travel all the way to the castle only to travel half-way back out to the fields.

## The Tourment at Wargem

Casimir beat Kamil, won 4,500 for the plate and horse

Caden enders a joust with Francesco  de Luna.

Caden wins his round. He opts to not absconded away with the other knight's plate

Casimir then fights Sir Philippe Montaigne, the recently knighted squire of Leon Blackwood. He treats him well after the win.Cas loses his third bout

Sir Thierry Dubois (Winner) Personal Guard of Duchess

### Archery Contest

Adruy, Lyla and Nathen Freehold participate in the archery contest. They all do well, some better than others, but over all - well.Lyla goes up against Emil the Red Spot and loses – Has a perfect shot the only one in the tourment.

### Squire Bout

Eloise wins the squire melee

Casimir talks with Philippe while Caden is quietly pissed, Because he also kills people for political reasons the same way that Cadens Master was killed.. They make a dinner date for a few days.

Maisy and Shiobon discuss the merits (or lack there of) of a Tournament. That with a simple slip, all lives become equal - king and squire - now left for worms. So why risk it? Then Maisy asks if Shiobon had any opinons on the Saffron Society. They discuss what Maisy's role in the Shiobhan's entourage. She would like Shiobhan to hire a tested to come alongside them, so she can help educate Maisy. In the meantime, she is going to find information for Shiobhan among the entourages.

Casismer and Lyla are talking and Eloise comes up and shows that she won her battles, and showing her reward, asking if Lyla is going to take on a squire?

Lady Agatha Bennet snuck into the inn and refused to answer Lyla or Casimir. After being manhaleded by Casimir she spoke finally to Shiobhan, finally introducing herself and inviting the group to dinner. No one saw her go in as she distracted them, and she slipped in. Casimir is very upset she just slipped in.

Caden pulls Peter and Siobhan aside to talk about ideas of peace

Lyla and Sovereign have a brief aside to discuss historical alliances and the shifting of the tides.

Conversations at dinner: Shiobhan chats with Emmrich Bennet, asking about Tonya and how she fairs, and a brief discussion on Tonya's mother. With information that the tested of Montimer make a point to have a child if they can before they get their 5th ring.
